1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org

```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Grafana Plugin Security Signature Verification

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement plugin signature verification: the plugin manifest signing, the signature validation on load, and the unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

65-assistanttext-
The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Plugin Signature Verification in Grafana

The implementation spans three main concerns:

### Manifest Signing (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`)
- `Signature.Calculate()` — main entry point; reads `MANIFEST.txt`, verifies PGP clearsign block, checks per-file SHA-256 hashes, validates plugin ID/version, and checks root URLs
- `Signature.Verify()` — performs the actual PGP signature verification using `openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature`
- `Signature.validateManifest()` — validates required manifest fields before crypto verification
- `verifyHash()` — SHA-256 file integrity check against manifest entries

### Signature Validation on Load (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`)
- `Validation.ValidateSignature()` — enforces policy: accepts valid/internal sigs, propagates parent signatures to nested plugins, and rejects invalid/modified ones; delegates unsigned plugin decisions to the authorizer

### Unsigned Plugin Allowlist (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`)
- `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin()` — allows unsigned plugins only in dev mode or when explicitly listed in `PluginsAllowUnsigned` (set via `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` in grafana.ini)

### Supporting infrastructure
- **Static key** (`statickey/static_retriever.go`): hardcoded Grafana Labs PGP public key
- **Dynamic key retriever** (`keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): fetches/caches keys from grafana.com API
- **Pipeline hooks** (`pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`, `pipeline/validation/steps.go`): wire the signature calculator and validator into the plugin loading pipeline
